-----title
长沙（潭州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='2338a4bd7b7a46c991f8dba75984dc71_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2338a4bd7b7a46c991f8dba75984dc71");'><span id='2338a4bd7b7a46c991f8dba75984dc71_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1174&endYear=1174')">1174年</a>　初赴省，别妾，有词。作品：《天仙子》（别酒醺醺容易醉）<div id='poem_85925' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85925' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85925?labeling=true' target='_blank'>天仙子<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>初赴省别妾</a><span class='authorDate'>（1174年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85925")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85925_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85925'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85925'>别酒醺醺容易醉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85925'>回过头来三十里。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85925'>马儿只管去如飞，牵一会。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85925'>坐一会。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85925'>断送杀人山共水。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85925_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85925'>是则青衫终可喜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85925'>不道恩情拚得未。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85925'>雪迷村店酒旗斜，去则是。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85925'>住则是。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85925_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85925'>烦恼自家烦恼你。</div><div id='poem_sentence_9_85925_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1175&endYear=1181')">1175-1181年</a>　在潭州游学。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1182&endYear=1182')">1182年</a>　三十岁前，读书漫游于江西、湖南，曾从戴溪游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1183&endYear=1183')">1183年</a>　在潭州获得参加次年春礼部大试资格。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
杭州（临安）
-----detail

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1202&endYear=1202')">1202年</a>　在临安，与郭倪等人交游，有诗。作品：嘉泰开乐日，殿岩泾原郭季端邀游凤山，自来美堂而上湖亭、海观、梅坡、石林，无不历览，最后登冲天楼，下介亭，观骑射歌舞，赋诗而归。<div id='poem_85910' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_4_85952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85952'>算整顿乾坤终有时。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85952_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85943' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85943?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁园春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span>卢蒲江席上，时有新第宗室</a><span id='poem_sentence_3_85943'>四举无成，十年不调，大宋神仙刘秀才。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85943'>如何好？<div id='poem_sentence_4_85943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85943'>将百千万事，付两三杯。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85943_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85943'>未尝戚戚于怀。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85943'>问自古英雄安在哉？<div id='poem_sentence_7_85943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85943'>任钱塘江上，潮生潮落；<div id='poem_sentence_8_85943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85943'>姑苏台畔，花谢花开。<div id='poem_sentence_9_85943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_85943'>盗号书生，强名举子，未老雪从头上催。<div id='poem_sentence_10_85943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_85943'>谁羡汝、拥三千珠履，十二金钗！</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_85943_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_85943'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(85943)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='bc3a539830ca4aeeb466d6076fe0c1cb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bc3a539830ca4aeeb466d6076fe0c1cb");'><span id='bc3a539830ca4aeeb466d6076fe0c1cb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>，53岁</div><div id='bc3a539830ca4aeeb466d6076fe0c1cb' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在临安，赋《西江月》词为韩侂胄祝寿。（堂上谋臣尊俎）<div id='poem_85937' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85937' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85937?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西江月</a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85937")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85937_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85937'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85937'>堂上谋臣尊俎，边头将士干戈。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85937'>天时地利与人和。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85937'>燕可伐欤曰可。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85937_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85937'>今日楼台鼎鼐，明年带砺山河。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85937'>大家齐唱大风歌。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85937'>不日四方来贺。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_85937_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_85937'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(85937)'>评注</a><span class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85926?labeling=true' target='_blank'>水龙吟<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85926_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85926'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85926'>庆流阅古无穷，相门又见生名世。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85926'>致君事业，全如忠献，经天纬地。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85926'>十二年间，挺身为国，勋庸知几。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85926'>便书之竹帛，铭之彝鼎，勤劳意、竟谁记。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85926_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85926'>一自平章庶政，觉人心、顿然兴起。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85926'>朝廷既正，乾坤交泰，华夷欢喜。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85926'>行定中原，锦衣归相，分茅□□。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85926_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85926'>看貂蝉绿鬓，中书上考，过三千岁。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_85926_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在临安，赋《念奴娇》词代寿韩侂胄。（玉带金鱼）<br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在临安，赋《满江红》词寿韩侂胄。（霜树啼鸦）<div id='poem_85987' class='_poem'><div id='poem_sentence_4_85987'>功甚大，心常小。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85987_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85987'>居廊庙，思<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_3_85947_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85947'>清泉怪石盘纡。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85947_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85947'>挥毫处，看淋漓雪壁，真草行书。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_85947_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ae10e7b4033045fc8c8cf4c2f4ab44b9_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ae10e7b4033045fc8c8cf4c2f4ab44b9");'><span id='ae10e7b4033045fc8c8cf4c2f4ab44b9_link' ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_996089")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_996089_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85988' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85988?labeling=true' target='_blank'>满江红<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span>高帅席上</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85988")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85988_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85988'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85988'>敌面风轻，一两点、海棠微雨。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85988'>春总在、英雄元帅，晓来游处。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85988'>楼阁万家<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_85988", 85988, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>帘幕</span>卷，江郊十里旌旗驻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85988'>有黄鹂、百舌啭新声，垂杨舞。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85988_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85988'>寒食近，喧箫鼓。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85988'>车马闹，铜鞮路。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85988'>尽不妨沈醉，与花为主。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85988'>风韵可将图画比，笑谈尽是惊人语。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85988'>问何如、邹湛岘山头，陪羊祜。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85988_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85988'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_85988_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>旅襄阳，有诗。作品：襄阳歌。<div id='poem_85919' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85919' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85919?labeling=true' target='_blank'>襄阳歌</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85919")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85919_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85919'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85919'>十年著脚走四方，胡不归来兮襄阳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85919'>襄阳真是用武国，上下吴蜀<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>天中央。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85919'>铜鞮坊里弓作市，八邑田熟麦当粮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85919'>一条路入秦陇去，落日彷佛见太行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85919'>土风沉浑士奇杰，呜呜酒后歌声发。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85919'>歌曰人定兮胜天，半壁久无胡日月。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85919'>买剑倾家赀，市马托生死。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85919'>科举非不好，行都兮万里。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85919'>人言边人尽粗材，卧龙高卧不肯来。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85919'>杜甫诗成米芾写，二三子亦英雄哉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_85919'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_85919_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_85919'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_85919_0'>⑴ 原作国，据四库本改</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_85919_comment'></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>旅襄阳，有诗寄友。作品：襄阳雪中寄江西诸友。<div id='poem_85807' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85807' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85807?labeling=true' target='_blank'>襄阳雪中寄江西诸友</a><span class='authorDate'>（1185年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85807")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85807_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85807'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85807'>雨涩风悭夜向阑，粉花飘扑客衣单。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85807_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85807'>功名有分平吴易，贫贱无闻访戴难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85807_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85807'>懒逐银杯行处马，静思玉鉴舞时鸾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85807_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85807'>诗成咫尺谁堪寄，当与邦人醉底看。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85807_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85807'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85807_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
武汉（武昌）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8f59427a6b4f4ce08b1172b9d5e06c67_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8f59427a6b4f4ce08b1172b9d5e06c67");'><span id='8f59427a6b4f4ce08b1172b9d5e06c67_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>，33岁</div><div id='8f59427a6b4f4ce08b1172b9d5e06c67' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过武昌，结识昌妓徐楚楚，有词。作品：《浣溪沙》（黄鹤楼前识楚卿）<span class='inlineComment2'>（作品参考曾荣耀《刘过与歌妓交游考论》，《郧阳高等师范专科学校学报》2008年2月，58页。）</span><div id='poem_85980' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85980' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85980?labeling=true' target='_blank'>浣溪沙<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>赠妓徐楚楚</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85980")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85980_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85980'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85980'>黄鹤楼前识楚卿。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85980'>彩云重叠拥娉婷。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85980'>席间谈笑觉风生。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85980_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85980'>标格胜如张好好，情怀浓似薛琼琼。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85980_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85980'>半帘花月听弹筝。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85980_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>武昌妓徐楚楚索题，赋词。作品：《西江月》（楼上佳人楚楚）<div id='poem_85940' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85940' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85940?labeling=true' target='_blank'>西江月<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span>武昌妓徐楚楚号问月索题</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85940")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85940_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85940'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85940'>楼上佳人楚楚，天边皓月徐徐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85940'>呼童忙为卷虾须。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85940'>试问中情几句。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85940_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85940'>圆少却因底事，缺多毕竟何如。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85940'>嫦娥无语谩踌躇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85940_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85940'>飞过画栏西去。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_85940_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
当涂
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='7bf5dae149934679afe40a7f780bbe2f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("7bf5dae149934679afe40a7f780bbe2f");'><span id='7bf5dae149934679afe40a7f780bbe2f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>，33岁</div><div id='7bf5dae149934679afe40a7f780bbe2f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　前往淮河边地，游八公山、采石矶，有诗。作品：舣舟采石。<div id='poem_85862' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85862' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85862?labeling=true' target='_blank'>舣舟采石</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85862")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85862_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85862'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85862'>我昔南游武昌夏口之山川，赤壁吊古齐安边。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85862'>又尝北抵鹤唳风声地，八公山前望淝水。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85862'>谁令舣舟牛渚矶，楼船蔽江忆当时。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85862'>周郎未战曹瞒走，谢安一笑苻坚危。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85862'>黄云如屯夜月白，箭痕刀痕满枯骨。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85862'>健儿饭饱饮马来，意气犹雄歌尚烈。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85862'>只今采石还戍兵，诸将奄奄泉下人。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85862'>饭囊盛饭酒瓮酒，位去三衙称好手<span class='inlineComment2'>（以上《龙洲道人诗集》卷一）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85862_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85862'></div><div id='poem_sentence_8_85862_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
盱眙
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='30bc311f52904c1f9818a17ba318d4f7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("30bc311f52904c1f9818a17ba318d4f7");'><span id='30bc311f52904c1f9818a17ba318d4f7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>，33岁</div><div id='30bc311f52904c1f9818a17ba318d4f7' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1186&endYear=1186')">1186年</a>　至盱眙，有诗。作品：盱眙行。<div id='poem_85855' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85855' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85855?labeling=true' target='_blank'>盱眙行</a><span class='authorDate'>（1186年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85855")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85855_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85855'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85855'>车徐行，马后驰，天寒游子来盱眙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85855'>功名邂逅未可知，生身毕竟要何为。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85855'>既不起<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作视）</span>草黄金闺，又不侍<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>宴白玉墀。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85855'>何不夜投将军飞<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作扉）</span>，劝上征伐鞭四夷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85855'>沧海可填山可移，男儿志气当如斯。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85855'>安能生死困毛锥，八韵作赋五字诗。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85855'>金牌郎君黄头儿，有眼不忍重见之。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85855'>志大才疏浩无期，逢人举似人笑嬉。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85855'>谓之痴人<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作儿）</span>未必痴，唤作奇士何能奇。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_85855_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_85855'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_2_85855_0'>⑴ 原作待，据四库本改，江湖集作陪</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_85855_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='82c33038e6c1440b906855a0d543ecc8_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("82c33038e6c1440b906855a0d543ecc8");'><span id='82c33038e6c1440b906855a0d543ecc8_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1206&endYear=1206')">1206年</a>，53岁</div><div id='82c33038e6c1440b906855a0d543ecc8' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>夏，开始北伐，以诗记从军。作品：从军乐。<div id='poem_85817' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85817' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85817?labeling=true' target='_blank'>从军乐</a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85817")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85817_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85817'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85817'>蛟龙宝剑鸊鹈刀，黄金络马花盘袍。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85817'>臂弓腰矢出门去，百战未怕皋兰鏖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85817'>酒酣纵猎自足快，诗成横槊人称豪。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85817'>但期处死<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作死处）</span>得其所，一死政自轻鸿毛<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作秋毫）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85817'>将军三箭定天山，丞相五月入不毛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85817'>生前封侯死庙食，云台突兀秋山高。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85817'>书生如鱼蠹书册，辛苦雕篆真徒劳。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85817'>儿时鼓箧走京国，渐老一第犹未叨。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85817'>自嗟赋命如纸薄，始信<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作知）</span>从军古云乐。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85817_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85817'></div><div id='poem_sentence_9_85817_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>见陈孝庆，有诗五首记录。作品：呈陈总领五首。<div id='poem_85844' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85844' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85844?labeling=true' target='_blank'>呈陈总领五首<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85844")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85844_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85844'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85844'>旄头欃枪锐冲击，杀气隆隆半天黑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85844'>千家悲哀万家哭，唐邓征魂招不得。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85844'>北斗移杓向西指，八月风高塞尘起。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85844'>大军忠义赴襄阳，飞鸟潜鱼未知死。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85844'>黔黎殷忧痛无策，愿得空中降韩白。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85844'>呜呼何代无奇才，世间未有黄金台。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85844_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85844'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_85844_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_85843' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85843' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85843?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85843_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85843'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85843'>太宗造唐刬隋乱，仁义结民过炎汉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85843_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85843'>胡雏负恩逆天纪，忠义回天四方起。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85843_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85843'>嗟哉主将失纪律，百万秦人半为鬼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85843_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85843'>浮云改变异今古，不谓前车眼中睹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85843_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85843'>尝时潼关说歌舒，今日襄阳说皇甫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85843_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85843'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_85843_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_85842' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85842' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85842?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85842_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85842'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85842'>先生文章擅经纬，战法渊源如孔子。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85842'>当时蜒獠沸溪洞，一扫蛮风净如水。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85842'>胸中气压万人将，亿万貔貅资馈饷。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85842'>汉家火德接天统，秘计奇谋堪任相。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85842'>愿公飞章告天子，敌疾如风走如鬼。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85842_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85842'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_85842_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_85841' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85841' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85841?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85841_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85841'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85841'>商蚷驰河河可凭，精卫填海海可平。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85841'>物情大忌不量力，立志亦复加专精。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85841'>忆昨痛哭丽正门，白袍黑帽如游魂。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85841'>中书堂留草茅疏，不赐诛戮光宗恩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85841'>暮年志气耻彫丧，广长阳中吊名将。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85841'>愿持上方三寸铁，细剖赤心告今上。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85841_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85841'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_85841_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_85840' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85840' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85840?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其五 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1206年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85840_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85840'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85840'>今上聪明过尧汤，师王忠纯如魏王。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85840'>君上戮力殄仇虏，六月戈甲飞冰霜。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85840'>泗州已复汉正朔，议饰寝庙修洛阳。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85840'>草茅蝼蚁百无用，山林岂复中原梦。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85840'>敬须洗眼候河清，读公浯水中兴颂。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85840_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85840'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_85840_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
长兴
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='33502a0511484f69b22d76466ca3eb1f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("33502a0511484f69b22d76466ca3eb1f");'><span id='33502a0511484f69b22d76466ca3eb1f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>，34岁</div><div id='33502a0511484f69b22d76466ca3eb1f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1187&endYear=1187')">1187年</a>　从北地南返，经湖州长兴，与程松有交。<br /></div>

-----title
和县（和州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='50316915b1854f7481cae6a6b0cc816f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("50316915b1854f7481cae6a6b0cc816f");'><span id='50316915b1854f7481cae6a6b0cc816f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>，37岁</div><div id='50316915b1854f7481cae6a6b0cc816f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1190&endYear=1190')">1190年</a>　是年有会试，从临安北上，到和州、焦湖一带。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='b4d077e2af6f4ce9a0f8ac0d9b977596_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b4d077e2af6f4ce9a0f8ac0d9b977596");'><span id='b4d077e2af6f4ce9a0f8ac0d9b977596_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年</a>，42岁</div><div id='b4d077e2af6f4ce9a0f8ac0d9b977596' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>重游淮甸，拜谒和州知州程九万，有文。作品：贺庐帅程徽猷鹏飞启。<div id='poem_1288441' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1288441' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1288441?labeling=true' target='_blank'>贺庐帅程徽猷鹏飞启</a><span class='authorDate'>（1195年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_1288441")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1288441_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1288441'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1288441'>升华徽阁，稳镇巨藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1288441_comment'></div>驾千里之舳舻，从天而下；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1288441_comment'></div>建十州之牙纛，易地则然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1288441_comment'></div>况睽违叔子之岘山，而指顾谢安之淝水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1288441_comment'></div>望历阳而入境，憩遗爱之甘棠；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1288441_comment'></div>道秋浦以过家，衣故乡之昼锦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1288441_comment'></div>功名鼎盛，福禄阶升。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1288441_comment'></div>父子同时，盖此豸冠之未有；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1288441_comment'></div>弟兄使虏，亦今雁塞之所无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1288441_comment'></div>譬犹全家白日以上天，何异万贯缠腰而骑鹤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1288441_comment'></div>所以欣欣而有喜，至于挈挈以远来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1288441_comment'></div>以贺而言，非辞可记。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1288441_comment'></div>恭惟某九华磅礴之气，大江汹涌之才。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1288441_comment'></div>自唐虞三代以来，无书不读；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1288441_comment'></div>除李杜数家之外，其诗最工。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1288441_comment'></div>虽决科续后于众人，而治县独名于一世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1288441_comment'></div>身处繁杂而不乱，移羽檄于莫容致诘之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1288441_comment'></div>变生仓卒而有谋，流货泉于不可得行之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1288441_comment'></div>非无馆阁进文字语言之职，亦有台省叙纠弹封驳之官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1288441_comment'></div>上念神州，久沦沙漠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1288441_comment'></div>蛇豕互为之吞噬，胡运寖衰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1288441_comment'></div>獭鹯未免于先驱，虏亡可待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1288441_comment'></div>欲以英雄之士，乘其机会之秋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1288441_comment'></div>故畀之亚父所封之城，而授以三国必争之地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1288441_comment'></div>矧合淝之所部，跨全楚之雄边。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1288441_comment'></div>若赤壁之得周郎，始名出将；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1288441_comment'></div>如中原之非祖逖，谁可渡江？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1288441_comment'></div>睿眷甚深，升除特异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1288441_comment'></div>要当收拾人才而尽用，庶几恢复境土以成功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1288441_comment'></div>三千馀年黄河之清，维其时矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1288441_comment'></div>二十四考中书之令，属之公乎！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1288441_comment'></div>某幸杖履之曾陪，阻门墙而益远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1288441_comment'></div>有书为患，几不容于天地之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1288441_comment'></div>无家可归，但落魄于江湖之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1288441_comment'></div>断绝帝乡之梦，辛勤淮甸之行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1288441_comment'></div>莫吹寒谷之笙竽，无复赏音之山水。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1288441_comment'></div>视文章为小技，久废语言；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1288441_comment'></div>悟富贵之傥来，甚安贫贱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1288441_comment'></div>然辱泥涂而自弃者，固士之不幸；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1288441_comment'></div>见华轩而颂美者，亦人之真情。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1288441_comment'></div>访杜甫于浣花溪边，尚冀严中丞之慷慨；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1288441_comment'></div>宴王勃于滕王阁上，犹希阎都督之风流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1288441_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_42_1288441_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在和州，寄诗赠程九万。作品：寄程鹏飞。<div id='poem_85760' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85760' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85760?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄程鹏飞</a><span class='authorDate'>（1195年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85760")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85760_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85760'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85760'>往事游边忆少年，未尝携刺五侯门。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85760'>春风跃马汉南道，落日椎牛淮上村。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85760'>科举未为暮年计，穷途不忍向人言。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85760'>男儿慷慨头当断，未有人施可报恩。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85760_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85760'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85760_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
南京（建康）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='51ee52c269344ac8bc5f74e97f6dd73d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("51ee52c269344ac8bc5f74e97f6dd73d");'><span id='51ee52c269344ac8bc5f74e97f6dd73d_link' id='poem_sentence_2_85589_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_85592' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85592' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85592?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85592'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85592'>绫衾厌入承明直，却把一麾江上来。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85592'>云气隔天迷望眼，不堪花落几宫槐。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85592_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85592'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_85592_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_85591' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85591' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85591?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85591'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85591'>夫子声名号浙西，作成文士欲何为。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85591'>达人胸次元无翳，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_85591", 85591, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>芥子须弥</span>我独知。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85591_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85591'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_85591_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_85593' color: gray;'>▪</span>在建康，与刘炜交，有诗二首。作品：上刘和州炜二首。<div id='poem_85810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85810?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_85651'>场经古战心欲折，客老诸侯饥更驱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85651_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85651'>去国寂寥从白眼，筹边谋画看洪<span id='poem_sentence_1_85790'>江淮浩渺洲渚没，凤鸟寂寥鸿雁来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85790_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85790'>时事不言惟拄笏，书生无用且衔杯。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85790_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85790'>生平自厌胸中窄，万里霜天一日开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85790_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85790'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85790_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游建康赏心亭，有诗。<div id='poem_85907' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85907' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85907?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赏心亭<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作赏心寺次胡仲方韵）</span></a><span /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85907_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85907'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85907'>尘襟抖擞风云入，石刻摩挲岁月流。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85907'>惆怅谪仙鸾驭远，离离别恨黯滩头<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作难收）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85907_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85907'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85907_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游建康白鹭洲，有诗。作品：观白鹭洲风涛。<span target='_blank'>观白鹭洲风涛</a><span class='authorDate'>（1190年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85696")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85696_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85696'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85696'>一声雷鼓挟风威，顷刻冲涛没钓矶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85696'>行客骇看银汉落，阳侯惊起玉山飞。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85696'>蛟龙便尔争先化，鸥鹭茫然失所依。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85696'>安得长竿入吾手，翩然东海钓鳌归。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85696_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85696'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85696_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='387491943bb649da807c6e3ad6eaa0ad_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("387491943bb649da807c6e3ad6eaa0ad");'><span id='387491943bb649da807c6e3ad6eaa0ad_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1200&endYear=1201')">1200-1201年</a>，47-48岁</div><div id='387491943bb649da807c6e3ad6eaa0ad' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1200&endYear=1200')">1200年</a>　与吴芳仲发生冲突，陷入金陵狱，有文上吴琚。作品：建康狱中上吴居父启。<div id='poem_1288437' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1288437' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1288437?labeling=true' target='_blank'>建康狱中上吴居父启<span class='inlineComment2'>（时魏杭广夫为秋官）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1200年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_1288437")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1288437_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1288437'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1288437'>范雎诈称张禄，盖有所谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1288437_comment'></div>少游即是太虚，别无他意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1288437_comment'></div>但可辨薰莸之有臭，不当使玉石之俱焚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1288437_comment'></div>辄摅屈抑之情，上渎神明之听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1288437_comment'></div>伏念某庐陵生长，湖海倦游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1288437_comment'></div>鼓行之老气不衰，嫉恶之刚肠犹在。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1288437_comment'></div>汉廷重贾太傅，上曾览积薪厝火之书；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1288437_comment'></div>江南有贺方回，人争诵芳草断肠之句。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1288437_comment'></div>敢期无谓，亦到有司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1288437_comment'></div>困一身于囹圄之中，不胜涂炭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1288437_comment'></div>被五木于拘挛之下，正值冰霜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1288437_comment'></div>累知己以并临，辱长须而下及。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1288437_comment'></div>若欲擢发而尽数其罪，亦有百口而莫辨其辜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1288437_comment'></div>横逆之来，哀鸣有以。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1288437_comment'></div>恭审某，官列三公之数，帅为诸道之尊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1288437_comment'></div>文翁阐儒教于蜀都，不闻著述；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1288437_comment'></div>常衮振文风于岭峤，所欠威名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1288437_comment'></div>唯道德之备，兼数者而有之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1288437_comment'></div>故位望之高，列诸藩而未已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1288437_comment'></div>金章茅土，与国同休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1288437_comment'></div>玉匮券书，其门益大。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1288437_comment'></div>此尚今时之间有，允为前世之所无。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1288437_comment'></div>公独一人，名高千古。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1288437_comment'></div>骨法寿天人之相，精神行地上之仙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1288437_comment'></div>不以身为将相，而敢忽于细微；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1288437_comment'></div>不以才兼文武，而尤勤于学问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1288437_comment'></div>性耽佳句，无非人间未见之诗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1288437_comment'></div>真草行书，更作天下不刊之字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1288437_comment'></div>尊君亲而弥敬，远形势而自疏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1288437_comment'></div>久为戚畹之范模，可作世家之龟鉴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1288437_comment'></div>有如庶狱，犹戒多门。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1288437_comment'></div>若吴芳仲平虎，委巷匪人，穷檐下走。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1288437_comment'></div>弃母亲而勿侍，冒国恤以图欢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1288437_comment'></div>挥买笑之金，动縻百万；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1288437_comment'></div>磨折簪之玉，苟合再三。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1288437_comment'></div>积威暴如虎狼，忽交游如虮虱。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1288437_comment'></div>鸩毒安宴，蛾眉痛心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1288437_comment'></div>但知浮花浪蕊之足欢，誓同穴死；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1288437_comment'></div>不悟冶叶倡条之微意，久欲钗分。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1288437_comment'></div>气一怒而火攻，军四驰而剑舞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1288437_comment'></div>凶焰有如此者，锋铓谁敢当哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1288437_comment'></div>韩擒虎在门，顾丽华而难恋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1288437_comment'></div>陶朱公有意，与西子以皆来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1288437_comment'></div>共掩其非，合污以利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1288437_comment'></div>枚数赦前之小过，历陈试后之虚名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1288437_comment'></div>苍生如谢安石何，事无诳取；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1288437_comment'></div>汝意识袁彦道否，王有假时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1288437_comment'></div>尚虞小人之多赀，或陷君子于不义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1288437_comment'></div>望水鉴致妍媸之察，使权衡无轻重之差。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1288437_comment'></div>曾参虽未尝杀人，疑信尚生于慈母；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1288437_comment'></div>赤壁若果然放火，踉跄亦走于阿瞒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1288437_comment'></div>况在陪都，实非细故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1288437_comment'></div>倘强横稍加于裁抑，则善良始可以保全。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1288437_comment'></div>邹生坐狱中而上言，始犹冤抑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1288437_comment'></div>召伯憩甘棠而听讼，终觊宽平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1288437_comment'></div>往此以还，未知攸措。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1288437_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1200&endYear=1200')">1200年</a>　在建康拜谒郭倪，有诗。作品：谒郭马帅倪。<div id='poem_85882' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85882' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85882?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒郭马帅<span class='inlineComment2'>（傀）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1200年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85882")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85882_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85882'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85882'>千金买骏马，百金<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作城）</span>市蛾眉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85882'>长安酒家楼，挥洒惊人诗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85882'>天子不得臣，公卿气吞之。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85882'>俯视儿女辈，自诡<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作揆）</span>男子奇。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85882'>谁知金陵都，五年重来兹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85882'>黑貂日以敝，尘埃鬓成丝。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85882'>故人风雨散，知己今为谁。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85882'>郭侯山西英，而有熊豹姿。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85882'>巍峨西忠庙，乔木人所思。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85882'>垂芳到云仍，大将奕世为。<div id='poem_sentence_9_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_85882'>兄弟各三衙，父子步武随。<div id='poem_sentence_10_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_85882'>万户侯冠军，金印何累累。<div id='poem_sentence_11_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_85882'>虽然平戎策，终郁未得施。<div id='poem_sentence_12_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_85882'>方今群胡扰，似觉虏运衰。<div id='poem_sentence_13_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_85882'>达靼军其西，会以蒙国斯。<div id='poem_sentence_14_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_85882'>蛇豕互吞噬，干戈极猖披。<div id='poem_sentence_15_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_85882'>盗贼毛猬起，敛民及<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作竭）</span>刀锥。<div id='poem_sentence_16_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_85882'>父老思汉官，壶浆傒王师。<div id='poem_sentence_17_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_85882'>吾君自神武，妙算出筹帷。<div id='poem_sentence_18_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_85882'>收揽天下才，尺寸不可遗。<div id='poem_sentence_19_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_85882'>机会一日来，恢复此其时。<div id='poem_sentence_20_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_85882'>况如郭侯者，礼贤正谦卑。<div id='poem_sentence_21_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_85882'>使之会云龙，列城归指麾。<div id='poem_sentence_22_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_85882'>安知古中原，不使同驱驰。<div id='poem_sentence_23_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_85882'>过也久沦落，狂名诸公知。<div id='poem_sentence_24_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_85882'>然亦壮心胆，志慕鞭四夷。<div id='poem_sentence_25_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_85882'>脱靴呼<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作奴）</span>将军，举扇障元规。<div id='poem_sentence_26_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_85882'>有音世不赏，诗酒聊自嬉。<div id='poem_sentence_27_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_85882'>霜风忽无情，一夜冷彻肌。<div id='poem_sentence_28_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_85882'>高卧百尺楼，闭门无晨炊。<div id='poem_sentence_29_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_85882'>起视匣中剑，依旧光陆离。<div id='poem_sentence_30_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_85882'>有恩或可报，一死所不辞。<div id='poem_sentence_31_85882_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_85882'></div><div id='poem_sentence_32_85882_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1201&endYear=1201')">1201年</a>　居金陵。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
仪征
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='11663de5e8cc4584a2083579327ae60d_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("11663de5e8cc4584a2083579327ae60d");'><span id='11663de5e8cc4584a2083579327ae60d_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>，38岁</div><div id='11663de5e8cc4584a2083579327ae60d' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>　由两淮转赴苏州，途经真州与许从道结拜。<br /></div>

-----title
苏州（长洲）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='1f169d7b49764ad999152e31bdec39ad_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("1f169d7b49764ad999152e31bdec39ad");'><span id='1f169d7b49764ad999152e31bdec39ad_link' id='poem_sentence_2_85663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85663'>尘埃俗吏那能此，一段奇功自可知。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85663_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85662'>十州已茂圜扉草，一炷初凝画戟香。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85662'>铜剖虎符新雨露，玉持使节旧风霜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85662_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85662'>明年樱笋成时候，不在乌台即玉堂。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85661'>山川形势今三辅，人物英雄古列侯。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85661_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85660'>适意秋风宁为鲙，惊心半夜忽闻钟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85660_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85659'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85659'>已办行都欲去船，个中因得少留连。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85659'>书生不愿悬金印，只觅扬州骑鹤钱。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85659_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85659'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85659_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在长洲拜见俞太古，有诗。作品：俞太古尝叩阍上书，有名天下，甚敬之，相会于姑苏，将归洞庭读书，赋诗以壮其行。<div id='poem_85860' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85860' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85860?labeling=true' </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85860")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85860_comment'></div><div class='titleComment'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_title_85860_0'>① 二字原作读旧书，据四库本改</div></div></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85860'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85860'>人树俱不堪，岁月驹隙过。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85860'>老怀泪如洗，欲唱谁当和。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85860'>洛阳今少年，弊事劳力破。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85860'>精神经百鍊，锋锐坚不挫。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85860'>陶名滋惟旧，攲席快一坐。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85860'>气焰九霄虹，磊落万玉货。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85860'>平生床上下，楼辄让子卧。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85860'>诸公吮疽尔，不去良可唾。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85860'>洞庭清风熟，肄业情勿惰。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85860'>有诗寄来者，工拙吾能课。<div id='poem_sentence_9_85860_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_85860'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_85860_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='80a60fae0171440885c0a35848c54a6e_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("80a60fae0171440885c0a35848c54a6e");'><span id='80a60fae0171440885c0a35848c54a6e_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1198')">1196-1198年</a>，43-45岁</div><div id='80a60fae0171440885c0a35848c54a6e' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1196&endYear=1196')">1196年</a>　庆元二年至四年，以苏州为中心游历，为俞灏建房作文。作品：排青轩上梁文。<span class='inlineComment2'>（《全宋文》该篇题目为《为吴县尉俞灏商卿作排青轩上梁文》，见《全宋文》290册第446页。）</span><div id='poem_1288446' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1288446' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1288446?labeling=true' target='_blank'>为吴县尉俞灏商卿作排青轩上梁文</a><span class='authorDate'>（1196年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_1288446")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1288446_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1288446'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1288446'>夫差国大，苏为吴、常、秀之尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1288446_comment'></div>东野官卑，尉处簿、参、丞之底。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1288446_comment'></div>觉身外之尘埃可见，奈胸中之风月自佳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1288446_comment'></div>爰葺西偏，未为左计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1288446_comment'></div>某精神玉雪，名誉斗山。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1288446_comment'></div>盖尝读万卷之书，不自意百夫之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1288446_comment'></div>凝香画戟，合寘之铃阁以哦诗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1288446_comment'></div>挝鼓水乡，今乃以儒官而警盗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1288446_comment'></div>纳须弥于芥子，坐涂炭于朝衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1288446_comment'></div>廨宇甚卑，难为展布；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1288446_comment'></div>园亭不治，无以游观。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1288446_comment'></div>稍仍旧之数椽，用作新于一宇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1288446_comment'></div>门洞然而尽辟，瓦鳞次而不飘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1288446_comment'></div>窗纸虚明，帘旌摇动。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1288446_comment'></div>湖山缭绕，著身图画之间；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1288446_comment'></div>竹桂阴森，揖客旌旗之下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1288446_comment'></div>体因居而寖大，心与地以俱平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1288446_comment'></div>遂伸作尉之腰，少试活人之手。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1288446_comment'></div>偶留十日，获见一斑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1288446_comment'></div>眉目娟娟，烟树浓妆之西子；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1288446_comment'></div>衣裳楚楚，荷花傅粉之六郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1288446_comment'></div>棋局留残，如行道院；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1288446_comment'></div>芸香剔蠹，似到馆中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1288446_comment'></div>撷莼菜以煮羹，款已归之张翰；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1288446_comment'></div>持蟹螯而荐酒，酌未醉之刘伶。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1288446_comment'></div>辄以从游，见之颂述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1288446_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_1288446'>东，子真端的有仙风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1288446_comment'></div>壶天留得春常在，脸上桃花非酒红。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1288446_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1288446'>西，莫憎此室尚卑栖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1288446_comment'></div>湖水渐平风浪退，一双鸂𪄠在清溪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1288446_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_1288446'>南，老子清贫旧已甘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1288446_comment'></div>若言富贵求而得，未必玉堂如草庵。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1288446_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_32_1288446'>北，胡运之衰今已极。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1288446_comment'></div>闭门使学草檄书，不可擒王止擒贼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1288446_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_34_1288446'>上，想见诗成更官样。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1288446_comment'></div>庭空吏散寂无人，消得行吟自筇杖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1288446_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_36_1288446'>下，扫地焚香作清夜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1288446_comment'></div>维摩丈室等虚空，不是寻常县官舍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1288446_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_38_1288446'>右，伏愿上梁之后，仙风不老，官职益高。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1288446_comment'></div>归直玉堂，对翻阶之红药；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1288446_comment'></div>独提椽笔，草拜相之白麻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1288446_comment'></div>云霄上乎九天，河海润乎千里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1288446_comment'></div>尚期他日，卧老夫于百尺之楼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1288446_comment'></div>何待来年，庇寒士乎万间之屋。</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1288446_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1197&endYear=1197')">1197年</a>　与常熟县令孙应时有交，有二诗相寄。作品：寄竹隐先生孙应时二首。<div id='poem_85872' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85872' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85872?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄竹隐先生孙应时<span class='inlineComment2'>（时为常熟宰）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1197年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85872")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85872_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85872'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85872'>苏州酒滴如真珠，公能醉之酒百壶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85872'>得閒政恐不来尔，来则倒屣相与俱。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85872'>江山绕楼诗句好，奔走万变同驰驱。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85872'>大书小草各有能<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作态）</span>，雷雹<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作电）</span>震耀莺花姝。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85872'>当其半醉尚醒在，宛若处女未嫁夫。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85872'>杯行到手湖海歇<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作竭）</span>，翻覆云雨来<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作成）</span>须臾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85872'>羲之屈使坐北面，命骚如役仆与奴。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85872'>角巾斜飘鬓毛出，笔墨颠倒衫袖乌。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85872'>回旋左右如有碍，归路不记长须扶。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85872'>宾侪指摘士窃笑，亦有好事描为图。<div id='poem_sentence_9_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_85872'>或云先生郁于用，浮沈欲以酒自娱。<div id='poem_sentence_10_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_85872'>实非能饮姑好客，不时斗酒由人须。<div id='poem_sentence_11_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_85872'>若予乃是真饮者，糟丘日日乡无何<span class='inlineComment2'>（原作何无，据四库本乙）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_12_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_85872'>虽然人亦难意料，未可目以为酒徒。<div id='poem_sentence_13_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_85872'>相逢摆<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作脱）</span>略边幅尽，胸次开豁无城郛。<div id='poem_sentence_14_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_85872'>敛藏穷达付<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作寄）</span>之酒，不以礼法自束拘。<div id='poem_sentence_15_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_85872'>情归一真举无伪，滑稽玩世为通儒。<div id='poem_sentence_16_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_85872'>饮与不饮无不可，醉醒醒醉同一区。<div id='poem_sentence_17_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_85872'>痴人之前莫说梦，梦中说梦愈阔迂。<div id='poem_sentence_18_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_85872'>客来辄饮饮辄醉，此其所以为竹湖。<div id='poem_sentence_19_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_85872'>不然他人岂无酒，欲去此脚自懒趋。<div id='poem_sentence_20_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_85872'>计公之客日百数，结束冠带纷座隅。<div id='poem_sentence_21_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_85872'>欲言喉牙物如梗，中怀腹非外示愚。<div id='poem_sentence_22_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_85872'>不如鄙性好诚实，退无取议<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作所攻）</span>进不谀。<div id='poem_sentence_23_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_85872'>欧公自爱曼卿放，昌黎亦喜刘叉粗。<div id='poem_sentence_24_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_85872'>满城风雨重阳近，黄花篱落金英敷。<div id='poem_sentence_25_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_26_85872'>山高凛风<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作风劲）</span>吹客倒，公楼虽小主者殊。<div id='poem_sentence_26_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_85872'>狂当相就取一醉，有酒饮我无酒酤。<div id='poem_sentence_27_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_85872'>此即<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作郎）</span>虽狂亦可喜，我去俗子畴当呼。<div id='poem_sentence_28_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_29_85872'>世无人兮<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作贺监）</span>亦已久，公不容我谁容乎。<div id='poem_sentence_29_85872_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_30_85872'></div><div id='poem_sentence_30_85872_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_85871' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85871' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85871?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄竹隐先生孙应时</a><span class='authorDate'>（1197年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85871")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85871_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85871'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85871'>竹湖人之英，剧县勇自试。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85871'>三年种桃李，遗爱及僮稚。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85871'>咸欲父母之，谓吾公之子。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85871'>独有督邮嫌，见谓不事事。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85871'>瑕疵催科细，欲以三尺治。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85871'>八月羁僦楼，半年縻隐市。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85871'>小窗天日晴，洒落自胸次。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85871'>抖擞旧尘埃，楮札左右置。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85871'>寄傲点画间，挥染当游戏。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85871'>人贤世所希，嗜好人共贵。<div id='poem_sentence_9_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_85871'>车马闹填门，载酒日纷至。<div id='poem_sentence_10_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_85871'>大书极豪放，小草亦姿媚。<div id='poem_sentence_11_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_85871'>敛藏经纶业，进此第一义。<div id='poem_sentence_12_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_85871'>玉板抄歌诗，石碑刻图记。<div id='poem_sentence_13_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_85871'>人家锦为轴，高壁垂至地。<div id='poem_sentence_14_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_85871'>袭藏较工拙，临写费同异。<div id='poem_sentence_15_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_85871'>争如老刘子，落魄一狂士。<div id='poem_sentence_16_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_85871'>半生不读书，颇能会其意。<div id='poem_sentence_17_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_85871'>寒泉骥马饮，平陆蛟龙起。<div id='poem_sentence_18_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_19_85871'>得非久幽愤，于以发奇气。<div id='poem_sentence_19_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_85871'>故使钟鼎疏，自足名一世。<div id='poem_sentence_20_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_21_85871'>毛锥久见绝，一见尚能喜。<div id='poem_sentence_21_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_85871'>酒边袖予诗，不誉亦不忌。<div id='poem_sentence_22_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_23_85871'>有时夺之去，箱箧馀故纸。<div id='poem_sentence_23_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_24_85871'>如持将军诰，屡博姑苏醉。<div id='poem_sentence_24_85871_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_85871'></div><div id='poem_sentence_25_85871_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　孙应时被贬官，刘过赋词纪事。作品：《沁园春》（问讯竹湖）<span class='inlineComment2'>（词调误作《念奴娇》，据《刘过年表》、《全宋词》改。）</span><div id='poem_85956' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85956' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85956?labeling=true' target='_blank'>沁园春<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其四 </span>寄孙竹湖</a><span class='authorDate'>（1198年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85956")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85956_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85956'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85956'>问讯竹湖，竹如之何，如何未归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85956'>道吴山越水，无非佳处，来无定止，去亦何之。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85956'>莫是秋来，未能忘耳，心与孤云相伴飞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85956'>愁无奈，但北窗寄傲，南涧题诗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85956_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85956'>人生万事成痴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85956'>算世上久无公是非。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85956'>恨云台突兀，无君子者，雪堂流落，有美人兮。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85956'>疏雨梧桐，微云河汉，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_85956", 85956, "Clauses/21/Comments/0")'>钟鼎山林</span>无限悲。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85956_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85956'>阳山县，是昌黎误汝，汝误昌黎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_85956_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　与许从道邂逅于苏州。<br /></div>
-----end



-----title
扬州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ddf5b9504080436e935e46baad0a6069_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ddf5b9504080436e935e46baad0a6069");'><span id='ddf5b9504080436e935e46baad0a6069_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>，38岁</div><div id='ddf5b9504080436e935e46baad0a6069' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1191&endYear=1191')">1191年</a>　秋冬之际，转赴扬州，有词。作品：《六州歌头》（镇长淮）<div id='poem_85922' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85922' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85922?labeling=true' target='_blank'>六州歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1191年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85922")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85922_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85922'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85922'>镇长淮，一都会，古扬州。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85922'>升平日，珠帘十里春风、小红楼。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85922'>谁知艰难去，边尘暗，胡马扰，笙歌散，衣冠渡，使人愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85922'>屈指细思，血战成何事，万户封侯。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85922'>但琼花无恙，开落几经秋。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85922'>故垒荒丘。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85922'>似含羞。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85922_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85922'>怅望金陵宅，丹阳郡，山不断<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_85922", 85922, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>绸缪</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85922'>兴亡梦，荣枯泪，水东流。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85922'>甚时休。<div id='poem_sentence_9_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_85922'>野灶<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_85922", 85922, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>炊烟</span>里，依然是，宿貔貅。<div id='poem_sentence_10_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_85922'>叹灯火，今萧索，尚淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_11_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_85922'>莫上醉翁亭，看濛濛雨、杨柳丝柔。<div id='poem_sentence_12_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_85922'>笑书生无用，富贵拙身谋。<div id='poem_sentence_13_85922_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_85922'>骑鹤东游。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_85922_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
宁波（庆元府）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='45f39103d6a24141b3e727097ede8deb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("45f39103d6a24141b3e727097ede8deb");'><span id='45f39103d6a24141b3e727097ede8deb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1192&endYear=1192')">1192年</a>，39岁</div><div id='45f39103d6a24141b3e727097ede8deb' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在庆元府参加秋试，观明州大阅，有诗。作品：明州观大阅。<div id='poem_85854' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85854' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85854?labeling=true' target='_blank'>明州观大阅</a><span class='authorDate'>（1192年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85854")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85854_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85854'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85854'>书生灯窗困毛锥，说著刀剑何时持。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85854'>不见拔山昔项羽，何必燕赵士始奇。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85854'>军容灿灿生光辉，悲风惨淡杀气怒，对此忽作边头思。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85854'>熊罴不哗晓争出，万骑驰突寒打围。<div id='poem_sentence_10_85854'>将军仰笑兵军贺，金帛填委深沟池。<div id='poem_sentence_10_85854_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_85854'>十年文穷坐百拙，感慨一赋从军诗。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_85854_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>在庆元府观明州大阅，赋词。作品：《念奴娇》（万马不嘶）<div id='poem_85957' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85957' 绍兴

-----title
建德（严州）
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='16d5a6cfb52f4d59974fcb034c22b5fa_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("16d5a6cfb52f4d59974fcb034c22b5fa");'><span id='16d5a6cfb52f4d59974fcb034c22b5fa_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>，40岁</div><div id='16d5a6cfb52f4d59974fcb034c22b5fa' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　由绍兴西去，入严州，有诗寄程准。作品：寄桐庐程宰。<div id='poem_85757' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85757' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85757?labeling=true' target='_blank'>寄桐庐程宰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85757")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85757_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85757'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85757'>路入严州去，桐庐得暂过。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85757'>盘餐汤饼贱，机杼绮罗多。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85757'>令尹哦诗治，居民酌酒歌。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85757'>吏人公事少，门雀可张罗。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85757_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85757'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85757_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
