-----title
歙县
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='e58e0dc9080740c1b028932b09e9d743_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("e58e0dc9080740c1b028932b09e9d743");'><span id='e58e0dc9080740c1b028932b09e9d743_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>，40岁</div><div id='e58e0dc9080740c1b028932b09e9d743' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1193&endYear=1193')">1193年</a>　至徽州，游歙溪，有诗。作品：入徽州。<div id='poem_85649' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85649' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85649?labeling=true' target='_blank'>入徽州</a><span class='authorDate'>（1193年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85649")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85649_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85649'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85649'>白傅庭前正解船，梦中忽已过番川。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85649'>红尘冉冉行天上，黄道骎骎近日边。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85649'>石洞歙溪俱可砚，山肥徽路总堪田。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85649'>把茅便欲侨居去，奈此功名未了缘。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85649_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85649'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85649_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
六合
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='0d0e7a637aec4e3b8d52141de4d73600_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("0d0e7a637aec4e3b8d52141de4d73600");'><span id='0d0e7a637aec4e3b8d52141de4d73600_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1195&endYear=1195')">1195年</a>，42岁</div><div id='0d0e7a637aec4e3b8d52141de4d73600' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>秋，北至六合等地，有诗。作品：六合道中。<div id='poem_85668' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85668' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85668?labeling=true' target='_blank'>六合道中</a><span class='authorDate'>（1195年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85668")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85668_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85668'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85668'>十年曾记此<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作此记）</span>来游，有策中原一战收。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85668'>蒲柳易凋嫌势去，金汤无用卒和休。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85668'>悲风髣髴鸣刁斗，缺月参差照敌楼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85668'>庙食封侯何日事，不堪老<span class='inlineComment2'>（江湖集作羸）</span>马又滁州。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85668_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85668'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85668_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>过六合，醉中赋诗。作品：醉中偶成。<div id='poem_85788' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85788' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85788?labeling=true' target='_blank'>醉中偶成</a><span class='authorDate'>（1195年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85788")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85788_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85788'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85788'>小院蒲萄月架东，舞腰忙趁鼓声雄。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85788'>诗成䌽笔分题后，人在金钗赌令中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85788'>秋叶冷吟风浩荡，晚林烘透日玲珑。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85788'>腰间若佩滁州印，定有人呼作醉翁。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85788_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85788'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85788_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
无锡
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b183352025fa4789aac96ec2c5437a5a_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b183352025fa4789aac96ec2c5437a5a");'><span id='b183352025fa4789aac96ec2c5437a5a_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>，45岁</div><div id='b183352025fa4789aac96ec2c5437a5a' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游无锡道观，有诗。<div id='poem_85670' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85670' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85670?labeling=true' target='_blank'>无锡道观</a><span class='authorDate'>（1198年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85670")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85670_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85670'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85670'>门外红尘市一廛，买瓜买李兴悠然。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85670'>树根石透月洒落，殿阁屋多风折旋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85670'>卖墨道人勤置酒，能诗老子欲飞仙。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85670'>髑髅南面蛆虫辈，鹏鴳逍遥各自天。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85670_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85670'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85670_comment'></div></div></div><br /><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>游无锡惠山，有诗。作品：雪晴游惠山。<div id='poem_85883' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85883' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85883?labeling=true' target='_blank'>雪晴游惠山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1198年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85883")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85883_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85883'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85883'>松杉如立密当门，长在山中管送迎。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85883'>栖石草根留雪在，响阶檐溜滴春声。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85883'>簿书拨置君能到，碑刻摩挲眼倍明。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85883'>欲作小诗无好句，只题年月记经行。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85883_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85883'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85883_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
吴江
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='9ddb3b8a6e2c4aed9561aaa69f1c0c63_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("9ddb3b8a6e2c4aed9561aaa69f1c0c63");'><span id='9ddb3b8a6e2c4aed9561aaa69f1c0c63_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>，45岁</div><div id='9ddb3b8a6e2c4aed9561aaa69f1c0c63' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1198&endYear=1198')">1198年</a>　过吴江，有诗。作品：泊船吴江县。<div id='poem_85718' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85718' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85718?labeling=true' target='_blank'>泊船吴江县</a><span class='authorDate'>（1198年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85718")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85718_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85718'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85718'>草树连塘岸，人家半橘洲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85718'>暖寒寻酒去，觉懒罢诗休。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85718'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_2_85718", 85718, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>逆境</span>年年梦，劳生处处愁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85718'>天涯倦行客，明日又苏州。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85718_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85718'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85718_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
东阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='16db9475e2e040e4a1f2a19f887d5e75_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("16db9475e2e040e4a1f2a19f887d5e75");'><span id='16db9475e2e040e4a1f2a19f887d5e75_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>，46岁</div><div id='16db9475e2e040e4a1f2a19f887d5e75' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年9月3日</a>　游东阳，访许从道，书信相通。作品：与许从道书。<span class='inlineComment2'>（许从道《东阳游戏序》）</span><div id='poem_1288443' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1288443' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1288443?labeling=true' target='_blank'>与许从道书</a><span class='authorDate'>（1199年9月3日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_1288443")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1288443_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1288443'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1288443'>九月初三日，友生庐陵刘过再拜致书从道省元足下：某不肖，属交下风几年矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1288443_comment'></div>倒指记之，自戊申及今己未，日月逾迈，动经一纪，君犹书生，我为布衣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1288443_comment'></div>呜呼，人生几十二年哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1288443_comment'></div>追念畴昔，定交于行都而盍簪于仪真，邂逅于金陵、姑苏，行路之难，中忧百罹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1288443_comment'></div>此如人饮水，冷煖自知，不可为他人言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1288443_comment'></div>他人读书，句读犹未通，把笔为文章，模拟窜窃；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1288443_comment'></div>粗晓声病，即取高第，为时达官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1288443_comment'></div>足下试于乡，于湖南、江东、两浙，仅能一再中，而姓名上礼部辄报罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1288443_comment'></div>某亦自计偕湖北之次，寂寞无闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1288443_comment'></div>此两人者，所谓天壤间无聊之人耳，交可以绝矣，而相知者益深。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1288443_comment'></div>嗜艾嚼蜡，计足下悬悬于某，已自有不可晓者，而况乎仆哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1288443_comment'></div>方珉隐先生教学于湖也，从游之士无虑数百人，然而获亲且近者亦不过六七人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1288443_comment'></div>执经疑难，争相雄强，是固岂肯以气下人者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1288443_comment'></div>足下于是时，独以《春秋》为诸生冠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1288443_comment'></div>先生持文衡其间，既示人以低昂轻重之公，诸生虽不敢以私议足下，而后来乃稍稍各以所长脱去场屋矣，而足下名犹隶于贡籍。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1288443_comment'></div>澹庵《题名》具存，每一读之，不胜龙猪之叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1288443_comment'></div>静言思之，先生岂欺予哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1288443_comment'></div>虽然，某亦岂受人欺者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1288443_comment'></div>诸老先生、缙绅公卿与夫博洽儒雅之士，至骚人墨客之流，某虽未造阃奥，亦尝涉其涯涘矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1288443_comment'></div>至有与其学而丑其所为，爱其辞章而不乐其行义，外刚内柔，首尾舛逆，往往貌是而心非之者皆是。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1288443_comment'></div>独于足下，退降俛伏之无他。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1288443_comment'></div>自言若是，则某亦自欺者，而并与足下欺之哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1288443_comment'></div>韩退之交游相识千百人，或以事闻，或以艺取，或喜其一善，或以其久故。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1288443_comment'></div>至于崔群，则独相与如骨肉兄弟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1288443_comment'></div>不知群何修饬，而能取重于退之如此哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1288443_comment'></div>盖足下之所挟甚能，使某犁然当于心者，有不独《春秋》三传而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1288443_comment'></div>其学正大，其文条畅而甚华，其议论闳阔深远而有馀味。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1288443_comment'></div>又深知古今之变、国家兴衰成败之数，与之谈及边亭障堠、战守形势，又有洞然而不骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1288443_comment'></div>且其性识明敏，不诡随雷同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1288443_comment'></div>初视之若毅然有不可犯之色，而其实和平乐易，善与人交，掩覆其所短，弥缝其所长。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1288443_comment'></div>乃如某者，落魄不检，诸所交游者莫不厌而恶之，怨怒嫉骂，丛至沓来。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1288443_comment'></div>足下恬不加恤，待之如初，某所以感激悲叹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1288443_comment'></div>其深相知者大略如此，而其不知者可胜道哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1288443_comment'></div>今年夏，偶来东阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1288443_comment'></div>东阳，足下之乡里。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1288443_comment'></div>某始获拜其亲，识其子弟，与其厚善者游。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1288443_comment'></div>详听审观，又知足下之处乡里者静重而寡合。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1288443_comment'></div>虽然，君贫于家，与某之穷于途者不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1288443_comment'></div>某唯一身上下，听其意之所适从，足下则不可也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1288443_comment'></div>足下客诸侯亦久矣，而卒无所成。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1288443_comment'></div>田园荒芜，亲老而食指众，言而听、唱而和者谁欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1288443_comment'></div>开心胸、济缓急者谁欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1288443_comment'></div>夫使我有所为而人实爱，开心见诚，通融有无，患难相济者，不徒尔也，必先豁然有以示人不疑，彼此两忘，然后木石顽朴者尚可感动，而况于有情哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1288443_comment'></div>今足下之才不患其少，某犹为足下不满者，器局似未甚开广，有所欲言者，辄惭恧退缩而不自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1288443_comment'></div>得非坐一贫贱，故戚戚忧愤，朝夕徬徨，若将有物以掣其肘者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1288443_comment'></div>此等意态，必能成病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1288443_comment'></div>范滂、郭林宗隐不违亲，贞不绝俗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1288443_comment'></div>足下盖尝尚论林宗而友之者，而欲隐贞而违亲绝俗，而抑姑取其名而忘其实乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1288443_comment'></div>某本非放纵旷达之士，垂老而无所成立，故一切取穷达贵贱死生之变，寄之杯酒，浩歌痛饮，旁视无人，意将有所逃者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1288443_comment'></div>于是礼法之徒始以狂名归之，某亦受而不辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1288443_comment'></div>比之足下孤介峻洁，视天下事皆不屑为者，岂不万万相远？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1288443_comment'></div>然某诚恐拘挛已甚，则近于自隘；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1288443_comment'></div>偏于执方，则所行必多滞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1288443_comment'></div>古之通材达人疑不如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1288443_comment'></div>某坦荡不羁，虽不可以为法，然而与足下不用于时均也，但差乐耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1288443_comment'></div>以吾之所有，易足下之所无，药其膏肓之疾而起之，亦朋友切磋琢磨之义也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1288443_comment'></div>昔杜征南有《左传》之癖，足下于《传》可谓通矣，岂亦有所癖耶？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1288443_comment'></div>正言程冬老丁未岁尉长兴时为某言：「今天下惟四常」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1288443_comment'></div>某闻其言而甚惊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1288443_comment'></div>冬老之言曰：夫妇、父子、兄弟、君臣，此四者不可易之道，独朋友一常为不讲，故曰惟四常。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1288443_comment'></div>由今观之，冬老致身云霄之上，某亦岂无半面之雅，而辱在泥涂，邈之如路人，朋友之道讲不讲，何人也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1288443_comment'></div>栖栖异乡，与足下两穷相值，他人尚何责哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1288443_comment'></div>秋风益高，车马戒涂，凄其此心，又未知足下于何岁年，会于何处，而试于何地，而得失为何如。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1288443_comment'></div>朋友一常，尚冀他日与足下共敦之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1288443_comment'></div>有怀千万，书不尽言，不宣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1288443_comment'></div>某再拜。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_65_1288443'></div><div id='poem_sentence_65_1288443_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　与许从道游东阳碧涵，有诗。作品：同许从道游碧涵。<div id='poem_85827' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85827' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85827?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同许从道游涵碧亭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1199年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85827")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85827_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85827'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85827'>犯暑日午来，坐到日落归。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85827'>松桂丛团团，竹光净晖晖。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85827'>乳窦成濯缨，绿染身上衣。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85827'>却倾所携酒，对酌老石矶。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85827'>幽鸟当歌者，荐以首山薇。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85827'>敛藏大千界，游戏麈尾挥。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85827'>寺门长安道，结束驷马肥。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85827'>醉乡访腥荤，屏风肉红围。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85827'>我亭不关锁，何人款柴扉。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85827'>掉臂樵担行，藤萝自烟霏。<div id='poem_sentence_9_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_85827'>古所谓迂阔，若此二子稀。<div id='poem_sentence_10_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_85827'>既非携娉婷，又乏玉鞍飞。<div id='poem_sentence_11_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_85827'>不知有何好，林泉少焉依。<div id='poem_sentence_12_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_85827'>境胜更著语，鬼神暗呵讥。<div id='poem_sentence_13_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_85827'>但知笑他人，不觉自己非。<div id='poem_sentence_14_85827_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_85827'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_85827_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　在东阳，与徐子容交，有文。作品：赠徐子容说。<div id='poem_1288444' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1288444' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1288444?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠徐子容说</a><span class='authorDate'>（1199年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_1288444")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1288444_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1288444'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1288444'>东阳山水之窟，其民健而善斗，其士大夫力学而有节气。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1288444_comment'></div>风声所树，大略如此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1288444_comment'></div>窃尝试以他县人才计之，在闽、浙间，未为极盛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1288444_comment'></div>倒指而数，由今文武两科而仕者三十馀人，比吾江西，亦云多矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1288444_comment'></div>然而通显于朝者寂寥而未闻，而名实孚于天下者亦罕见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1288444_comment'></div>推原其由，岂非世家少而师道不立之故欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1288444_comment'></div>国朝韩、吕，以元勋厚德居河之北、山之东，其后硕大繁衍，散而四方，多至百胄而千甲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1288444_comment'></div>彼非皆习训诂，尽业文章，盖其文献典刑深入肌骨，故子孙感其化，见之设施。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1288444_comment'></div>□□河汾，当隋末扰攘之秋，英伟隽特之士困伏草莽，无以自见。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1288444_comment'></div>王氏从容义理，相与房、杜、姚、薛辈优柔厌饫于诗书礼乐之中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1288444_comment'></div>一旦李唐勃兴，时人景从，以功业发身者其门子弟居半。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1288444_comment'></div>呜呼，此岂区区口舌论说者所能致哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1288444_comment'></div>吾友徐子容，此邦之著姓也，其兄弟子侄亦浸有贵者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1288444_comment'></div>今又移以其道淑诸人，开门授业徒，户外履满。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1288444_comment'></div>此宜某之所加敬而不敢窃议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1288444_comment'></div>今犹续进是说，岂非王谢子弟贵乎见闻，以退之而为师，且有位卑之羞欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1288444_comment'></div>吾观子容，质直而甚文，和易而有节，此可以师者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1288444_comment'></div>其徒有能自经义词赋之外以吾说推之，则谋王断国之论，致君泽民之业，出将入相之才，莅官行德之方，他日之所成就当不止此，毋徒曰吾计止应科举、图官职而已耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1288444_comment'></div>年日月，刘生说。</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1288444_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　寄徐东阳诗。作品：喜雨寄徐东阳。<div id='poem_85729' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85729' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85729?labeling=true' target='_blank'>春雨寄徐东阳</a><span class='authorDate'>（1199年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85729")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85729_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85729'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85729'>和州昔有贤从事，今作东阳父母官。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85729'>百里望风皆畏易，四郊得雨及时难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85729'>秋成有望米价减，水满不争民业安。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85729'>诗句定多公事少，不妨閒写寄人看。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85729_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85729'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85729_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　在东阳，作诗赠许从道之子。作品：赠许从道之子祖孙。<div id='poem_85917' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85917' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85917?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠许从道之子祖孙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1199年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85917")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85917_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85917'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85917'>祖孙今年几年齿，两髻紞紞垂到耳。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85917'>读书要以六经先，次第汉唐十七史。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85917'>老夫之见窃不然，别有一说为举似。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85917'>方今孽胡日衰甚，河朔早暮风尘起。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85917'>腐儒酸寒作何用，国家所欠奇伟士。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85917'>丈夫立身两字尽，臣子忠孝而已矣。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85917'>吾观汝相头面阔，颜色粗厚黑而紫。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85917'>汝翁七十鬓发转，汝父科第迟如此。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85917'>与生<span class='inlineComment2'>（四库本作君）</span>生死蠹文字，土田官人村夫子。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85917'>不如左弯右挟弓，肉食封侯差快耳。<div id='poem_sentence_9_85917_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_85917'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_85917_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1199&endYear=1199')">1199年</a>　在东阳，往来清潭山谷间，盘薄邑里，作绝句十首。作品：游清潭吕资益蟠谷十绝。<div id='poem_85902' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85902' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_85902_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85902'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85902'>一潭清净水<span class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85636'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85636'>逶迤路逐惊蛇去，转盼不知身已高。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85636_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' 江湖集作云木万重</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_85636_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_85631' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85631' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_title_85631_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85631'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85631'>野花红白倚岩开，只可<span class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85628'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85628'>老子垂垂秋露下，九月空山天气寒。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85628'>黄花剩开且勿剪，留得一秋烟雨看。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85628_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85628'></div><div id='poem_sentence_2_85628_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_85632' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85632' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85632?labeling=true' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85773'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85773'>使君人物旧乌台，天听虽高力挽回。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85773'>湖水欲平江为退，秋田未旱雨朱来。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85773'>云随黄鹤游何许，风满南楼亦快哉。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85773'>凉意入秋清可画，月岩知有桂花开。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85773_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85773'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85773_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_85772' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85772' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85772?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1204年）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>七言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_85772_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85772'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85772'>黄鹤山前雨乍过，城南草市乐如何。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85772'>千金估客倡楼醉，一笛牧童牛背歌。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85772'>江夏水生归未得，武昌鱼美价无多。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85772'>掉船亦欲徜徉去，古井而今淡不波。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85772_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85772'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_85772_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年</a>　武昌岳鄂王庙，赋词。作品：《六州歌头》（中兴诸将）<div id='poem_85923' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85923' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85923?labeling=true' target='_blank'>六州歌头<span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其一 </span>题岳鄂王庙</a><span class='authorDate'>（1204年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85923")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85923_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85923'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85923'>中兴诸将，谁是万人英？<div id='poem_sentence_0_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85923'>身草莽，人虽死，气<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_85923", 85923, "Clauses/4/Comments/0")'>填膺</span>，尚如生。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85923'>年少起河朔，弓两石，剑三尺，定襄汉，开虢洛，洗洞庭。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85923'>北望帝京，狡兔依然在，良犬先烹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85923'>过旧时营垒，荆鄂有遗民。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85923'>忆故将军，泪如倾。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85923_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85923'>说当年事，知恨苦：不奉诏，伪耶真？<div id='poem_sentence_6_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85923'>臣有罪，陛下圣，可<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_7_85923", 85923, "Clauses/25/Comments/0")'>鉴临</span>，一片心。<div id='poem_sentence_7_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_85923'>万古分茅土，终不到，旧奸臣。<div id='poem_sentence_8_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_85923'>人世夜，白日照，忽开明。<div id='poem_sentence_9_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_85923'>衮佩冕圭百拜，九泉下、荣感君恩。<div id='poem_sentence_10_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_85923'>看年年三月，满地野花春，卤簿迎神。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_85923_comment'></div></div><div class='poemComment' id='poem_comment_85923'><a href='javascript: ShowPoemComment(85923)'>评注</a><span class='inlineComment4'>（点击查看或隐藏评注）</span></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1204&endYear=1204')">1204年</a>　在武昌，赋词送湖北招抚吴猎。作品：《八声甘州》（问紫岩去后汉公卿）<div id='poem_85920' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_85920' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/85920?labeling=true' target='_blank'>八声甘州 送湖北招抚吴猎</a><span class='authorDate'>（1204年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 南宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(25192, "南宋", "刘过", "poem_title_85920")'>刘过</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_85920_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_85920'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_85920'>问紫岩去后汉公卿，不知几貂蝉。<div id='poem_sentence_0_85920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_85920'>谁能借留侯箸，著祖生鞭。<div id='poem_sentence_1_85920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_85920'>依旧尘沙万里，河洛染腥膻。<div id='poem_sentence_2_85920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_85920'>谁识道山客，衣钵曾传。<div id='poem_sentence_3_85920_comment'></div></div><br /><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_85920'>共记玉堂对策，欲先明大义，次第<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_85920", 85920, "Clauses/10/Comments/0")'>筹边</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_85920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_85920'>况重湖八桂，袖手已多年。<div id='poem_sentence_5_85920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_85920'>望中原驰驱去也，拥十州、牙纛正<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_85920", 85920, "Clauses/14/Comments/1")'>翩翩</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_85920_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_85920'>春风早，看东南王气，飞绕星躔。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_85920_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end
